<div id="u_nav">
    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

data-tn-section="about"><h1 class="cmp-section-first-header">About Medtronic</h1><div class="cmp-section clearfix cmp-about-description" data-tn-component="about-description"><p class="cmp-body-text"><span id="cmp-short-description">Founded in 1949 as a repair shop for medical devices, Medtronic has grown to become one of the largest healthcare technology companies in the world.  The recent integration of Covidien as the company&#39;s Minimally Invasive Therapies group allows Medtronic to expand the business and bring its services to even more people around the world. The company operates</span><span id="cmp-more-link-container">&nbsp;&ndash;&nbsp;<a href="javascript:void(0);" id="cmp-more-link" data-tn-action-click data-tn-element="more-link">more...</a></span>&nbsp;<span id="cmp-more-description" class="hidden">through three additional groups: Restorative Therapies Group, Cardiac and Vascular Group, and Diabetes Group. Medtronic operates in more than 140 countries.<br><br>Medtronic offers company matching on employee 401(k) contributions, and two weeks paid time off in the first year of employment. Many employees think the health insurance coverage is excellent, including &quot;amazing infertility treatment&quot; on the company&#39;s plans. Workers also like the &quot;friendly and inclusive work environment,&quot; the &quot;great work-life balance,&quot; and the fact that Medtronic &quot;invests heavily in training and developing&quot; its employees. However, some find that &quot;with the acquisition of Covidien, benefits have suffered a bit,&quot; though that is &quot;to be expected&quot; because of the fact that the company &quot;doubled in size.&quot;&nbsp;&ndash;&nbsp;<a href="javascript:void(0);" id="cmp-less-link">less</a></span></p></div><ul class="cmp-photo-stream" data-tn-component="about-photos"><li data-tn-element="photo[]"><a function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

    <script>

function regExpEscape(s) {
    return String(s).replace(/([-()\[\]{}+?*.$\^|,:#<!\\])/g, '\\$1').
            replace(/\x08/g, '\\x08');
}


function appendParamsOnce(url, params) {
    var useParams = params.replace(/^(\?|\&)/, '');
    if (url.match(new RegExp('[\\?|\\&]' + regExpEscape(useParams))) == null) {
        return url += (url.indexOf('?') > 0 ? '&' : '?' ) + useParams;
    }
    return url;
}

</script>

		    var grid = null;
		    var timer = null;
		    var gridpaneloaded = false;
		    var splitter = null;
		    var splitterresizing = false;
		    //This value indicates the description pane is resized for the first time or not
		    var firsttime = true;
		    
		    //Variable setting the expiry days of the cookie stored
		    var m_expire_days = 30; 
		    
		    var ShowMenuFlag = true;
		    
            var pageCount = 0;
		    
		    var bKeyDown  = true;
		    
		    var lastScrollPosition = 0;
		    
		    var bFirst = true;
		    
		    var bShowGridUpdateProgress  = false;
		    var bShowReadingPaneProgress = false;
		    
		    var bAddToBasketClicked = false;
		    
		    var m_nSelectedIndex = 0;
		    
            var GridCreated = function( sender )
            {          
                grid = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid";
                
                var masterTable = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).get_masterTableView();
                
                pageCount = parseInt( masterTable.get_pageCount() );
                if( pageCount > 1 )
                    ResizeAfterResponse();
                else
                    Resize();
                //timer = window.setInterval("RefreshSelectedRow()", 300);
                RefreshSelectedRow();
                //Fix the size of the grid after it is created. Added to fix grid resizing issue after sorting and grouping
                if( document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid_GridData" ) != null )
                {
                    document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid_GridData" ).className = "SearchResultsGridGridData";
                }
                
                //Set the expand-collapse column width in mozilla firefox 3.0.5 and above to fix the widening of grid columns
                if( navigator.userAgent.indexOf( "Firefox/3" ) != ( -1 ) )
                {
                    var arr = navigator.userAgent.split( "/" );
                    if( ( arr[arr.length-1].length == 3 ) && ( arr[arr.length-1] == '3.0' ) )
                    {
                        //Browser is firefox 3.0 not apply the fix
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        try
                        {
                            grid.MasterTableView.ColGroup.Cols[0].style.width = "10px";
                            var x = document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid_ctl01_Header" );
                            x.getElementsByTagName( 'colgroup' )[0].Cols[0].style.width = "10px";
                        }
                        catch( e )
                        {/*alert("catch");*/}
                    }
                } 
                setscrollbar();
            }
            
	    	var GridKeyDown = function( e )
	    	{
	    	    var masterTable = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).get_masterTableView();
	    	    m_nSelectedIndex = masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0]._itemIndexHierarchical;
	    	    //alert(masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].getDataKeyValue("ID"));
	    	    
                var retValue = true;
                var key      = window.event ? e.keyCode : e.which;

                if( key == 38 || key == 40 )
                {	    	        
	    	        bShowReadingPaneProgress = true;
                    bShowGridUpdateProgress  = false;
                    bKeyDown = true;
                
                    if( key == 40 )
                    {
                        if( m_nSelectedIndex != masterTable.get_dataItems().length - 1 )
                        {
                            masterTable.get_dataItems()[m_nSelectedIndex].set_selected(false);
                            m_nSelectedIndex = parseInt(m_nSelectedIndex) + 1;
                            
                            masterTable.get_dataItems()[m_nSelectedIndex].set_selected(true); 
                            SetCookie( "SelectedIndex", m_nSelectedIndex, m_expire_days );
                            __doPostBack( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid", m_nSelectedIndex );
                            //To implement Google Analytics Event Tracking for Job 'View' When user selects the Job with the KeyBoard shortcuts.
                             if(typeof _gaq != 'undefined')
                             {
                                
                                var jobID=masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].getDataKeyValue("ID");
                                var jobTitle=masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].getDataKeyValue("JobTitle");
                                
                                _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Job', 'View', jobID +' - '+ jobTitle]);
                             }
                             
                            retValue = false;
                       }
                    }

                    if( key == 38 )
                    {
                        if( m_nSelectedIndex != 0 ) 
                        {
                           masterTable.get_dataItems()[m_nSelectedIndex].set_selected(false);
                           m_nSelectedIndex = parseInt(m_nSelectedIndex) - 1;
                           masterTable.get_dataItems()[m_nSelectedIndex].set_selected(true); 
                           SetCookie( "SelectedIndex", m_nSelectedIndex, m_expire_days );
                           __doPostBack( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid", m_nSelectedIndex );
                            //To implement Google Analytics Event Tracking for Job 'View' When user selects the Job with the KeyBoard shortcuts.
                           if(typeof _gaq != 'undefined')
                           {
                                var jobID=masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].getDataKeyValue("ID");
                                var jobTitle=masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].getDataKeyValue("JobTitle");
                                
                                _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Job', 'View', jobID +' - '+ jobTitle]);
                           }
                           
                           retValue = false;
                        }
                    }
                    setscrollbar();
                    SetLastScrollPosition();
                    return false;
                }
                return true;
            }
            
            function setscrollbar()
            {
                //Setting scroll position
                var grid = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" );
                var masterTable = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).get_masterTableView();
                if ( masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0] )
                {
                    var rowElement = masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].get_element();
                    //get the main table scrollArea HTML element
                    var scrollArea = grid.GridDataDiv;
                    if( scrollArea )
                    {
                        if( bKeyDown )
                        {
                            //check if the selected row is below the viewable grid area
                            if( ( rowElement.offsetTop - scrollArea.scrollTop ) + rowElement.offsetHeight + 20 > scrollArea.offsetHeight )
                            {
                                //scroll down to selected row
                                scrollArea.scrollTop = scrollArea.scrollTop + ( rowElement.offsetTop - scrollArea.scrollTop ) + ( rowElement.offsetHeight - scrollArea.offsetHeight ) ;
                                lastScrollPosition = scrollArea.scrollTop + ( rowElement.offsetTop - scrollArea.scrollTop ) + ( rowElement.offsetHeight - scrollArea.offsetHeight ) ;
                                                
                            }
                            //chck if the selected row is above the viewable grid area
                            else if( ( rowElement.offsetTop - scrollArea.scrollTop ) < 0 )
                            {
                                //scroll the selected row to the top
                                scrollArea.scrollTop = rowElement.offsetTop;
                                lastScrollPosition = rowElement.offsetTop;
                            }
                            bKeyDown = false;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            scrollArea.scrollTop = lastScrollPosition;
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                SetFocusToGrid();
            }
            
            
	    		    
            var RefreshSelectedRow = function()
            {
                try
                {
                    var masterTable = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).get_masterTableView();
                    
                    if( ( masterTable.get_dataItems().length > 0 ) )
                    {
                        var nSelectedIndex = getCookie( "SelectedIndex" );
                        if( nSelectedIndex )
                        {
                            m_nSelectedIndex = nSelectedIndex;
                            
                            if( parseInt( m_nSelectedIndex ) <= parseInt( masterTable.get_dataItems().length ) )
                            {
                                if( 0 != masterTable.get_selectedItems().length )
                                {
                                    masterTable.get_dataItems()[ masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0]._itemIndexHierarchical ].set_selected( false );
                                }
                                masterTable.get_dataItems()[ m_nSelectedIndex ].set_selected( true );
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                if( 0 != masterTable.get_selectedItems().length )
                                {
                                    masterTable.get_dataItems()[ masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0]._itemIndexHierarchical ].set_selected( false );
                                }
                                m_nSelectedIndex = 0;
                                masterTable.get_dataItems()[ m_nSelectedIndex ].set_selected( true );
                                SetCookie( "SelectedIndex", m_nSelectedIndex, m_expire_days );
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            masterTable.get_dataItems()[m_nSelectedIndex].set_selected( true );
                            SetCookie( "SelectedIndex", m_nSelectedIndex, m_expire_days );
                        }
                    }
                    setscrollbar();
                }
                catch(err)
                {
                    setTimeout( "RefreshSelectedRow()", 300 );
                }
            }

            var RowClicked = function( sender, args )
            {
                SetLastScrollPosition();
                            
                m_nSelectedIndex = args.get_itemIndexHierarchical();
                //alert(m_nSelectedIndex);
                SetCookie( "SelectedIndex", m_nSelectedIndex ,m_expire_days );
                
                bShowReadingPaneProgress = true;
                bShowGridUpdateProgress = false;
                __doPostBack( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid", m_nSelectedIndex );
                //To implement Google Analytics Event Tracking for Job 'View' When user click the job.
                if(typeof _gaq != 'undefined')
                {
                    var jobID=args.getDataKeyValue("ID");
                    var jobTitle=args.getDataKeyValue("JobTitle");
                    _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Job', 'View', jobID +' - '+ jobTitle]);
                }
            }   

            var RowContextMenu = function ( sender, e )
            {
                if( ShowMenuFlag == true )
                {                    
                    var evt = e.get_domEvent();
                    
                    var masterTable = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).get_masterTableView();

                    var menu = ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_GridContextMenu;
                    menu.Items[0].SetValue( 'GridContext' );
                    menu.Items[1].SetValue( 'GridContext' );
                    menu.Items[2].SetValue(' GridContext' );
                    menu.Show( evt );
                }              
            }

            var ShowMenu = function ()
            {
                var menu = ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_GridContextMenu;
                menu.Items[0].SetValue( 'ReadingPaneContext' );
                menu.Items[1].SetValue( 'ReadingPaneContext' );
                menu.Items[2].SetValue( 'ReadingPaneContext' );
                
                var Flag = "False";
                if( Flag == "True" )
                {
                    menu.ShowAt( document.body.clientWidth - 165, WindowHeight() - GetNeededBodyHeight() - 7 );
                }
                else
                {
                    menu.ShowAt( document.body.clientWidth - 165, WindowHeight() - GetNeededBodyHeight() + 30 );    
                }
            }

            var gridpaneresized = function( sender )
            {
                //fix sizing again
                Resize();
                if( gridpaneloaded )
                {
                    //Store the width of the pane in cookie when it is resized.
                    SetCookie( sender.get_id(), sender.get_width(), m_expire_days );
                }
                gridpaneloaded = true;             
            }
            
            //The following two functions prevent the gridpane from resizing while resizing the window.
            //Before resizing the splitter set the minimum and maximum width of gridpane as current width and height
            var splitterbeforeresize = function( sender, eventArgs )
            {
                splitterresizing = true;
                if ( eventArgs.get_newWidth() != null )
                {
                    var middlePaneWidth = sender.getStartPane().get_width();
                    var middlePane = sender.getStartPane(); //retrieve the middle pane
                    middlePane.set_minWidth( middlePaneWidth ); //set minWidth = current Width --> no decrease
                    middlePane.set_maxWidth( middlePaneWidth ); //set maxWidth = current Width --> no increase
                }
                
            }
            
            //After the splitter is resized, set the minimum and maximum width to defaults to enable resizing
            var splitterresized = function( sender, eventArgs )
            {
                var middlePane = sender.getStartPane();
                middlePane.set_minWidth( 200 ); //set to minimum value: minWidth = 200
                middlePane.set_maxWidth( 10000 ); //set to default value: maxWidth = 10.000
                splitterresizing = false;
                if( !firsttime )
                {
                    adjustlastpanewidth( 1 );
                }
            }
            
             //Setting the width of the panes after the splitter is loaded
            var SplitterLoaded = function( sender )
            {
                if( sender )
                {
                    splitter = sender;
                }
                
                if( bFirst )
                {
                    var prm = Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance();
                    prm.add_initializeRequest( InitializeRequest );
                    prm.add_endRequest( EndRequest );
                    bShowGridUpdateProgress = true;
                    bShowReadingPaneProgress = true;
                    document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_updatepnlReadingPane" ).style.display = "none";
                    document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_updatepnlGrid" ).style.display = "none";
                    bFirst = false;
                }
                
                SetApplyViaEmailLink();
                SetFocusToGrid();
            }
            
            function sendajaxrequest()
            {
                __doPostBack( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid", "" );
            }
            
            var DescriptionPaneResized = function( sender )
            {
                if( !splitterresizing )
                {
                    if( firsttime )
                    {
                        adjustlastpanewidth( 2 );
                        firsttime = false;
                    }
                }
                
                if( pageCount > 1)
                    ResizeAfterResponse();
                else
                    Resize();
            }
            
            var adjustlastpanewidth = function( addtowidth )
            {
                if( splitter )
                {   
                    var endpane = splitter.getPaneByIndex( 2 );
                    var secondpane = splitter.getPaneByIndex( 1 );
                    try
                    {
                        secondpane.setVarSize( secondpane.getVarSize() + addtowidth );
                    }
                    catch( err )
                    {
                    }
                }
            }
            
            //This function is for closing the radmenu while resizing the splitter
            var panegridbeforeresize = function()
            {
                var menu = ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_GridContextMenu;
                menu.Show( false );
                menu.Hide();
            }
            
            var MenuItemClick = function( sender, args )
            {
                bShowGridUpdateProgress = false;
                
				//Added on 10-02-2009 
                //When the 'Apply Now' menu item is clicked it shows an alert -
                //only if the Apply Via Email is configured for the portal.
                if( ( args.Item.Text == "Apply Now" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "FR-Apply Now" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "Postulez dès maintenant" ) )
                {
                    var Flag = "False";
                    if( Flag == "True" )
                    {
                    
                        ShowSendMailMessage();

                    }
                    else
                    {
                        
                    }
                }
				//Modified on 10\02\09
                //openradwindow() function is used for open a radwindow while clicking "Tell a Friend" menu
                 if( ( args.Item.Text == "Share this Job" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "FR-Share this Job" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "En parler à un ami" ) ||(args.Item.Text == "(F)Share this Job") )           
                {
                     openradwindow('radwindow','#286FAC','SharethisJob.aspx',490,185,'Tell_a_friend.gif',args.Item.Text);
                     //OpenPopupWindow( 'SendToFriend.aspx', 695, 460 );
                     ///OpenPopupWindow( 'SharethisJob.aspx', 500, 180 );
                }
                 //openradwindow() function is used for open a radwindow while clicking "Printable View" menu
                if( ( args.Item.Text == "Printable View" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "FR-Printable View" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "Aperçu avant impression" ) )
                {
                    //openradwindow('radwindow','#286FAC','JobPrintPreview.aspx',890,600,'job16_info.gif','Job Details');
                    OpenPopupWindow( 'JobPrintPreview.aspx', 750, 550 );
                }
                
                if( ( args.Item.Text == "Add to Basket" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "FR-Add to Basket" ) || ( args.Item.Text == "Ajouter au panier" ) )
                {
                    bAddToBasketClicked = true;
                }
            }
			
			function ShowSendMailMessage()
            {
               alert( 'If you have an email client like Outlook installed on your computer, an email will now open automatically so you can apply with your current resume. If you are using a web mail client, see the detailed instructions at the bottom of the job description with information on how to apply by email.' );
               //To Implement Google Analytics Script When Apply Via Email Without Registering Checked.
                var masterTable = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).get_masterTableView();
                        if(typeof _gaq != 'undefined')
                             {
                                
                                var jobID=masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].getDataKeyValue("ID");
                                var jobTitle=masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0].getDataKeyValue("JobTitle");
                                
                                _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Job', 'Apply', jobID +' - '+ jobTitle]);
                             }
            }
            
            function InitializeRequest( sender, args ) 
            {   
                try
                {
                    ShowMenuFlag = false;
                    
                    RefreshSelectedRow();
                    setscrollbar();
                    
                    if( bShowReadingPaneProgress )
                        document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_updatepnlReadingPane" ).style.display = "none";
                    
                    if( bShowGridUpdateProgress )
                        document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_updatepnlGrid" ).style.display = "none";
                }
                catch(err)
                {
                }
            }
            
            function EndRequest( sender, args )
            {
                RefreshSelectedRow();
                if( args._response._aborted )
                {
                    return;
                }
                else
                {
                    SetApplyViaEmailLink();
                    
                    if( bShowReadingPaneProgress )
                    {
                        document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_updatepnlReadingPane" ).style.display = "block";
                        bShowReadingPaneProgress = false;
                    }
                    
                    if( bShowGridUpdateProgress )
                    {
                        document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_updatepnlGrid" ).style.display = "block";
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        bShowGridUpdateProgress = true;
                    }
                    
                    //fix sizing again
                    if( pageCount > 1)
                        ResizeAfterResponse();
                    else
                        Resize();
                    
                    setscrollbar();
                    
                    try
                    {
                        var err = args.get_error();
                        if ( err != null && ( ( err.name == 'Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManagerTimeoutException' )||( err.name == "Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManagerServerErrorException" ) ) )
                        {
                            args.set_errorHandled( true );
                        }
                    }
                    catch( eeee )
                    {
                    }
                }
                SetFocusToGrid();
                
                if( bAddToBasketClicked == true )
                {
                    bAddToBasketClicked = false;
                    bShowGridUpdateProgress = false;
                    window[ "ctl00_NavigationControl_NavigationPanelRadAjaxManager" ].ajaxRequest( "" );                    
                }
                
                ShowMenuFlag = true;
            }
            
            function ColumnResized()
            {
                if( pageCount > 1 )
                    ResizeAfterResponse();
                else
                    Resize();
            }
            
            function SetFocusToGrid()
            {
                try
		        {
	                var griddata = document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" );
	                
	                if( griddata != null )
	                {
	                    document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).focus();
	                }
	                
		            var element = document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid_GroupPanel" );
		            if( element != null )
		            {
		                document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid_GroupPanel" ).focus();
		            }
		        }
		        catch(e)
		        {
		        }
            }
            
            function SetApplyViaEmailLink()
            {
                try
                {
                    var Flag = "False";

                    if( Flag == "True" )
                    {
                        
                        document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_GridContextMenu_m0" ).href = document.getElementById( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_hiddenlabel" ).value;
                    }
                }
                catch(e)
                {
                }
            }
            
            function SetLastScrollPosition()
            {
                try
                {
                    var grid = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" );
                    var masterTable = $find( "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder_SearchResultsGrid" ).get_masterTableView();
                    if ( masterTable.get_selectedItems()[0] )
                    {
                        //get the main table scrollArea HTML element
                        var scrollArea = grid.GridDataDiv;
                        if( scrollArea )
                        {
                            lastScrollPosition = scrollArea.scrollTop;
                        }
                    }
                }
                catch(e)
                {
                }
            }
            
            function SetScrollAfterGrouping()
            {
                bKeyDown  = true;                        
                setscrollbar();
            }
            
            function SetAddToBasketStatus()
            {
                bAddToBasketClicked = true;
                bShowGridUpdateProgress = false;
            }
